train_df: pd.DataFrame, valid_df: pd.DataFrame) -> Optional[Dict]:\n   220→        \"\"\"Run a single fold of walk-forward validation. Returns metrics dict or None.\"\"\"\n   221→        X_train = train_df[self.feature_names]\n   222→        y_train = train_df[\"target\"]\n   223→        X_valid = valid_df[self.feature_names]\n   224→        y_valid = valid_df[\"target\"]\n   225→        valid_ohlc = valid_df[['close', 'high', 'low']]\n   226→        close_prices = valid_df[\"close\"]\n   227→\n   228→        # Re-score on validation set using profit_factor\n   253→        for i, ind in enumerate(pop.individuals):\n   254→            if ind.fitness is None or ind.fitness <= -1000:\n   255→                continue\n   256→            try:\n   257→                pred_valid = ind.model.predict(X_valid, threshold=0.5)\n   258→                if isinstance(pred_valid, np.ndarray):\n   259→                    pred_valid = pd.Series(pred_valid, index=X_valid.index)\n   260→                signals_ind = pred_valid.reindex(close_prices.index).fillna(-1).astype(int)\n   261→                self.trader.run(signals_ind, valid_ohlc)\n   262→                ind.fitness = self.trader.metrics.get('profit_factor', 0.0)\n   263→                ind.validation_metrics = self.trader.metrics\n   264→                print(f\"  Model {i+1}: profit_factor={ind.fitness:.4f}\", flush=True)\n   265→            except Exception as e:\n   266→                print(f\"  Rescoring error: {e}\", flush=True)\n   267→                ind.fitness = -1000.0\n   268→\n   269→        top_models = pop.get_diverse_best(n=5)\n   270→        self._log_feature_importances(top_models[0] if top_models else None)\n   271→\n   272→        # Generate consensus signals\n   273→        consensus = ConsensusGate(\n   274→            min_models_agree=ConsensusConfig.MIN_MODELS_AGREE,\n   275→            min_confidence=ConsensusConfig.MIN_CONFIDENCE\n   276→        )\n   277→        signals = consensus.decide(top_models, X_valid)\n   278→\n   279→        # Run simulator\n   280→        self.trader.run(signals, valid_ohlc)\n   281→        metrics = self.trader.metrics.copy()\n   282→\n   283→        # Directional accuracy\n   284→        mask = (signals != -1) & y_valid.notna()\n   285→        if mask.any():\n   286→            metrics[\"accuracy\"] = (signals[mask] == y_valid[mask]).mean()\n   287→        else:\n   288→            metrics[\"accuracy\"] = 0.0\n   289→\n   290→        print(f\"Fold result: accuracy={metrics['accuracy']:.4f}, bets/month={metrics.get('bets_per_month', 0):.2f}, \"\n   291→              f\"trades={metrics.get('n_trades', 0)}, sharpe={metrics.get('sharpe', 0):.3f}\", flush=True)\n   292→        return metrics\n   293→\n   294→    def run_walk_forward(\n   295→        self,\n   296→        df: pd.DataFrame\n   297→    ) -> Dict[str, float]:\n   298→        \"\"\"\n   299→        Run 2-fold walk-forward validation with non-overlapping validation windows.\n   300→        Fold 1 (earlier): validates on [T-2v, T-v]; Fold 2 (latest): validates on [T-v, T].\n   301→        Returns weighted-average metrics across folds for robust OOS estimation.\n   302→        \"\"\"\n   303→        print(\"Running multi-fold walk-forward validation...\", flush=True)\n   304→\n   305→        df_sorted = df.sort_values(\"open_time\").reset_index(drop=True)\n   306→        val_rows = int(ValidationConfig.VALID_DAYS * 24 * 60 / 15)\n   307→        total_rows = len(df_sorted)\n   308→\n   309→        if total_rows < val_rows + ValidationConfig.MIN_TRAIN_SAMPLES:\n   310→            print(\"Insufficient data for walk-forward.\", flush=True)\n   311→            return {\"accuracy\": 0.0, \"bets_per_month\": 0.0, \"n_folds\": 0}\n   312→\n   313→        # Determine how many non-overlapping folds fit (up to 3)\n   314→        n_folds = 1\n   315→        if total_rows >= 2 * val_rows + ValidationConfig.MIN_TRAIN_SAMPLES:\n   316→            n_folds = 2\n   317→        if total_rows >= 3 * val_rows + ValidationConfig.MIN_TRAIN_SAMPLES:\n   318→            n_folds = 3\n   319→\n   320→        fold_metrics = []\n   321→        for fold_idx in range(n_folds):\n   322→            # fold_idx=0 (earlier), fold_idx=1 (most recent)\n   323→            valid_end = total_rows - (n_folds - 1 - fold_idx) * val_rows\n   324→            valid_start = valid_end - val_rows\n   325→\n   326→            if valid_start < ValidationConfig.MIN_TRAIN_SAMPLES:\n   327→                print(f\"Fold {fold_idx+1}: insufficient train samples, skipping.\", flush=True)\n   328→                continue\n   329→\n   330→            valid_df = df_sorted.iloc[valid_start:valid_end].copy()\n   331→            train_df = df_sorted.iloc[:valid_start].copy()\n   332→\n   333→            if len(train_df) > ModelConfig.MAX_TRAIN_SAMPLES:\n   334→                train_df = train_df.tail(ModelConfig.MAX_TRAIN_SAMPLES).copy()\n   335→\n   336→            print(f\"\\nFold {fold_idx+1}/{n_folds}: train={len(train_df)}, valid={len(valid_df)}\", flush=True)\n   337→\n   338→            m = self._run_fold(train_df, valid_df)\n   339→            if m:\n   340→                fold_metrics.append(m)\n   341→\n   342→        if not fold_metrics:\n   343→            return {\"accuracy\": 0.0, \"bets_per_month\": 0.0, \"n_folds\": 0}\n   344→\n   345→        n = len(fold_metrics)\n   346→        total_trades = sum(m.get('n_trades', 0) for m in fold_metrics)\n   347→\n   348→        if total_trades == 0:\n   349→            combined = fold_metrics[-1].copy()\n   350→            combined[\"n_folds\"] = n\n   351→            return combined\n   352→\n   353→        # Aggregate: weighted accuracy by n_trades, average everything else\n   354→        accuracy = sum(m['accuracy'] * m.get('n_trades', 1) for m in fold_metrics) / total_trades\n   355→        combined = {\n   356→            \"accuracy\": accuracy,\n   357→            \"bets_per_month\": sum(m.get('bets_per_month', 0) for m in fold_metrics) / n,\n   358→            \"sharpe\": sum(m.get('sharpe', 0) for m in fold_metrics) / n,\n   359→            \"profit_factor\": sum(m.get('profit_factor', 0) for m in fold_metrics) / n,\n   360→            \"total_return\": sum(m.get('total_return', 0) for m in fold_metrics),\n   361→            \"max_drawdown\": max(m.get('max_drawdown', 0) for m in fold_metrics),\n   362→            \"n_trades\": total_trades,\n   363→            \"n_folds\": n,\n   364→        }\n   365→\n   366→        print(f\"\\nMulti-fold combined ({n} folds): accuracy={combined['accuracy']:.4f}, \"\n   367→              f\"bets/month={combined['bets_per_month']:.2f}, Sharpe={combined['sharpe']:.3f}, \"\n   368→              f\"total_return={combined['total_return']:.4f}, trades={total_trades}\", flush=True)\n   369→        return combined\n   370→\n   371→    def train_best_models(\n   372→        self,\n   373→        df: pd.DataFrame,\n   374→        population: Population,\n   375→        horizon_data: dict = None\n   376→    ):\n   377→        \"\"\"\n   378→        Train the best models on full recent data and optionally train horizon ensembles.\n   379→        \"\"\"\n   380→        print(\"Training best models on full data...\", flush=True)\n   381→\n   382→        # Returns metrics dict or None.\"\"\"\n        X_train = train_df[self.feature_names]\n        y_train = train_df[\"target\"]\n        X_valid = valid_df[self.feature_names]\n        y_valid = valid_df[\"target\"]\n        valid_ohlc = valid_df[['close', 'high', 'low']]\n        close_prices = valid_df[\"close\"]\n\n        # Train fresh population on this fold's training data\n        pop = Population(\n            population_size=ModelConfig.POPULATION_SIZE,\n            model_types=ModelConfig.MODEL_TYPES,\n            mutation_rate=ModelConfig.MUTATION_RATE,\n            crossover_rate=ModelConfig.CROSSOVER_RATE,\n            elitism_count=ModelConfig.ELITISM_COUNT\n        )\n        pop.initialize(input_dim=X_train.shape[1], feature_names=self.feature_names)\n\n        for gen in range(ModelConfig.GENERATIONS_PER_ITERATION):\n            for ind in pop.individuals:\n                try:\n                    ind.model.fit(X_train, y_train)\n                    pred = ind.model.predict(X_train, threshold=0.5)\n                    ind.fitness = (pred == y_train).mean()\n                except Exception as e:\n                    print(f\"    Training error: {e}\", flush=True)\n                    ind.fitness = -1000.0\n            if gen < ModelConfig.GENERATIONS_PER_ITERATION - 1:\n                pop.evolve()\n            best = pop.get_best(1)[0]\n            print(f\"    Gen {gen+1}: best_train_fitness={best.fitness:.4f} ({best.model_type})\", flush=True)\n\n        # Re-score on validation set using profit_factor\n        for i, ind in enumerate(pop.individuals):\n            if ind.fitness is None or ind.fitness <= -1000:\n                continue\n            try:\n                pred_valid = ind.model.predict(X_valid, threshold=0.5)\n                if isinstance(pred_valid, np.ndarray):\n                    pred_valid = pd.Series(pred_valid, index=X_valid.index)\n                signals_ind = pred_valid.reindex(close_prices.index).fillna(-1).astype(int)\n                self.trader.run(signals_ind, valid_ohlc)\n                ind.fitness = self.trader.metrics.get('profit_factor', 0.0)\n                ind.validation_metrics = self.trader.metrics\n                print(f\"  Model {i+1}: profit_factor={ind.fitness:.4f}\", flush=True)\n            except Exception as e:\n                print(f\"  Rescoring error: {e}\", flush=True)\n                ind.fitness = -1000.0\n\n        top_models = pop.get_diverse_best(n=5)\n        self._log_feature_importances(top_models[0] if top_models else None)\n\n        # Generate consensus signals\n        consensus = ConsensusGate(\n            min_models_agree=ConsensusConfig.MIN_MODELS_AGREE,\n            min_confidence=ConsensusConfig.MIN_CONFIDENCE\n        )\n        signals = consensus.decide(top_models, X_valid)\n\n        # Run simulator\n        self.trader.run(signals, valid_ohlc)\n        metrics = self.trader.metrics.copy()\n\n        # Directional accuracy\n        mask = (signals != -1) & y_valid.notna()\n        if mask.any():\n            metrics[\"accuracy\"] = (signals[mask] == y_valid[mask]).mean()\n        else:\n            metrics[\"accuracy\"] = 0.0\n\n        print(f\"Fold result: accuracy={metrics['accuracy']:.4f}, bets/month={metrics.get('bets_per_month', 0):.2f}, \"\n              f\"trades={metrics.get('n_trades', 0)}, sharpe={metrics.get('sharpe', 0):.3f}\", flush=True)\n        return metrics\n\n    def run_walk_forward(\n        self,\n        df: pd.DataFrame\n    ) -> Dict[str, float]:\n        \"\"\"\n        Run 2-fold walk-forward validation with non-overlapping validation windows.\n        Fold 1 (earlier): validates on [T-2v, T-v]; Fold 2 (latest): validates on [T-v, T].\n        Returns weighted-average metrics across folds for robust OOS estimation.\n        \"\"\"\n        print(\"Running multi-fold walk-forward validation...\", flush=True)\n\n        df_sorted = df.sort_values(\"open_time\").reset_index(drop=True)\n        val_rows = int(ValidationConfig.VALID_DAYS * 24 * 60 / 15)\n        total_rows = len(df_sorted)\n\n        if total_rows < val_rows + ValidationConfig.MIN_TRAIN_SAMPLES:\n            print(\"Insufficient data for walk-forward.\", flush=True)\n            return {\"accuracy\": 0.0, \"bets_per_month\": 0.0, \"n_folds\": 0}\n\n        # Determine how many non-overlapping folds fit (up to 3)\n        n_folds = 1\n        if total_rows >= 2 * val_rows + ValidationConfig.MIN_TRAIN_SAMPLES:\n            n_folds = 2\n        if total_rows >= 3 * val_rows + ValidationConfig.MIN_TRAIN_SAMPLES:\n            n_folds = 3\n\n        fold_metrics = []\n        for fold_idx in range(n_folds):\n            # fold_idx=0 (earlier), fold_idx=1 (most recent)\n            valid_end = total_rows - (n_folds - 1 - fold_idx) * val_rows\n            valid_start = valid_end - val_rows\n\n            if valid_start < ValidationConfig.MIN_TRAIN_SAMPLES:\n                print(f\"Fold {fold_idx+1}: insufficient train samples, skipping.\", flush=True)\n                continue\n\n            valid_df = df_sorted.iloc[valid_start:valid_end].copy()\n            train_df = df_sorted.iloc[:valid_start].copy()\n\n            if len(train_df) > ModelConfig.MAX_TRAIN_SAMPLES:\n                train_df = train_df.tail(ModelConfig.MAX_TRAIN_SAMPLES).copy()\n\n            print(f\"\\nFold {fold_idx+1}/{n_folds}: train={len(train_df)}, valid={len(valid_df)}\", flush=True)\n\n            m = self._run_fold(train_df, valid_df)\n            if m:\n                fold_metrics.append(m)\n\n        if not fold_metrics:\n            return {\"accuracy\": 0.0, \"bets_per_month\": 0.0, \"n_folds\": 0}\n\n        n = len(fold_metrics)\n        total_trades = sum(m.get('n_trades', 0) for m in fold_metrics)\n\n        if total_trades == 0:\n            combined = fold_metrics[-1].copy()\n            combined[\"n_folds\"] = n\n            return combined\n\n        # Aggregate: weighted accuracy by n_trades, average everything else\n        accuracy = sum(m['accuracy'] * m.get('n_trades', 1) for m in fold_metrics) / total_trades\n        combined = {\n            \"accuracy\": accuracy,\n            \"bets_per_month\": sum(m.get('bets_per_month', 0) for m in fold_metrics) / n,\n            \"sharpe\": sum(m.get('sharpe', 0) for m in fold_metrics) / n,\n            \"profit_factor\": sum(m.get('profit_factor', 0) for m in fold_metrics) / n,\n            \"total_return\": sum(m.get('total_return', 0) for m in fold_metrics),\n            \"max_drawdown\": max(m.get('max_drawdown', 0) for m in fold_metrics),\n            \"n_trades\": total_trades,\n            \"n_folds\": n,\n        }\n\n        print(f\"\\nMulti-fold combined ({n} folds): accuracy={combined['accuracy']:.4f}, \"\n              f\"bets/month={combined['bets_per_month']:.2f}, Sharpe={combined['sharpe']:.3f}, \"\n              f\"total_return={combined['total_return']:.4f}, trades={total_trades}\", flush=True)\n        return combined\n\n    def train_best_models(\n        self,\n        df: pd.DataFrame,\n        population: Population,\n        horizon_data: dict = None\n    ):\n        \"\"\"\n        Train the best models on full recent data and optionally train horizon ensembles.\n        \"\"\"\n        print(\"Training best models on full data...\", flush=True)\n\n        # Use recent data (last N days) for final training\n        recent_days = 60\n        cutoff_time = df[\"open_time\"].max() - timedelta(days=recent_days)\n        recent_df = df[df[\"open_time\"] >= cutoff_time].copy()\n        print(f\"Recent training data: {len(recent_df)} samples\", flush=True)\n\n        X_recent = recent_df[self.feature_names]\n        y_recent = recent_df[\"target\"]\n\n        # Get top models\n        top_models = population.get_diverse_best(n=ConsensusConfig.MIN_MODELS_AGREE + 2)\n        print(f\"Selected {len(top_models)} top models for retraining\", flush=True)\n\n        # Retrain on full recent data\n        for i, ind in enumerate(top_models):\n            try:\n                print(f\"  Retraining model {i+1}/{len(top_models)} ({ind.model_type})\", flush=True)\n                ind.model.fit(X_recent, y_recent)\n                print(f\"    Done\", flush=True)\n            except Exception as e:\n                print(f\"  Failed to train {ind.model_type}: {e}\", flush=True)\n\n        # Use correct horizon minutes: factor * 15 minutes\n                    horizon_minutes = factor * 15\n                    df_horizon = resample_to_horizon(recent_df, horizon_minutes, factor)\n                    print(f\"    Resampled to {len(df_horizon)} rows\", flush=True)\n                    if len(df_horizon) > 100:\n                        df_horizon = create_target(df_horizon, forward_periods=1)\n                        df_horizon = add_technical_indicators(df_horizon)\n                        df_horizon = add_regime_features(df_horizon)\n                        df_horizon = df_horizon.dropna()\n                        print(f\"    Prepared {len(df_horizon)} samples with {len(df_horizon.columns)} features\", flush=True)\n                        horizon_data[h_name] = df_horizon\n                self.horizon_ensemble.fit_horizon_models(horizon_data, y_recent)\n                print(\"Horizon ensemble training complete\", flush=True)\n            else:\n                print(\"No additional horizons to train (HORIZONS only includes 15m)\", flush=True)\n        else:\n            self.horizon_ensemble.fit_horizon_models(horizon_data, y_recent)\n\n        self.main_population = population\n        self.top_models = top_models\n\n    def generate_current_signals(\n        self,\n        current_features: pd.DataFrame,\n        use_horizon: bool = True\n    ) -> pd.Series:\n        \"\"\"\n        Generate trading signals for the most recent data points.\n        \"\"\"\n        if self.top_models is None:\n            raise RuntimeError(\"Models not trained. At least MIN_MODELS_AGREE models must agree on direction\n    - Average confidence must exceed MIN_CONFIDENCE\n    \"\"\"\n\n    def __init__(\n        self,\n        min_models_agree: int = ConsensusConfig.MIN_MODELS_AGREE,\n        min_confidence: float = ConsensusConfig.MIN_CONFIDENCE\n    ):\n        self.min_models_agree = min_models_agree\n        self.min_confidence = min_confidence\n\n    def decide(\n        self,\n        models: List[Individual],\n        X: pd.DataFrame\n    ) -> pd.Series:\n        \"\"\"\n        Generate final trading signals (UP=1, DOWN=0, NO_TRADE=-1).\n\n        Args:\n            models: list of trained model individuals\n            X: feature DataFrame to predict on\n\n        Returns:\n            Series of signals (1, 0, or -1) aligned to X.index\n        \"\"\"\n        signals = pd.Series(index=X.index, data=0)\n        probas_matrix = []\n\n        for ind in models:\n            try:\n                proba = ind.model.predict_proba(X)\n                probas_matrix.append(proba)\n            except Exception as e:\n                continue\n\n        if not probas_matrix:\n            # No model worked, all NO_TRADE\n            signals[:] = -1\n            return signals\n\n        probas_array = np.array(probas_matrix)  # shape: (n_models, n_samples)\n\n        # Average confidence for each sample\n        avg_proba = probas_array.mean(axis=0)\n\n        # Count models predicting UP\n        up_votes = (probas_array >= 0.5).sum(axis=0)\n\n        down_votes = len(probas_matrix) - up_votes\n\n        # Apply gating rules\n        for i, (avg_p, up, down) in enumerate(zip(avg_proba, up_votes, down_votes)):\n            # Check agreement\n            if up >= self.min_models_agree:\n                direction = 1\n                confidence = avg_p\n            elif down >= self.min_models_agree:\n                direction = 0\n                confidence = 1 - avg_p  # confidence in DOWN is 1 - avg_proba\n            else:\n                signals.iloc[i] = -1\n                continue\n\n            # Check confidence threshold\n            if confidence >= self.min_confidence:\n                signals.iloc[i] = direction\n            else:\n                signals.iloc[i] = -1\n\n        return signals\n\n    def adjust_thresholds(\n        self,\n        recent_performance: Dict[str, float],\n        target_sharpe: float = 1.0,\n        target_profit_factor: float = 1.2,\n        target_accuracy: float = 0.65,\n        target_bets: float = 90.0\n    ):\n        \"\"\"\n        Dynamically adjust consensus thresholds based on recent performance.\n\n        Prioritizes risk-adjusted returns (Sharpe) and profitability (profit factor).\n        If Sharpe or profit factor are below target, tighten thresholds to improve quality.\n        If accuracy is high but Sharpe is low, also tighten (filter out low-quality trades).\n        If bets are too low and accuracy acceptable, loosen to increase frequency.\n        \"\"\"\n        sharpe = recent_performance.get(\"sharpe\", -1000.0)\n        profit_factor = recent_performance.get(\"profit_factor\", 0.0)\n        accuracy = recent_performance.get(\"accuracy\", 0.5)\n        bets_per_month = recent_performance.get(\"bets_per_month\", 0.0)\n\n        # If we already have sufficient accuracy and activity, avoid tightening thresholds\n        # which could zero out trading. This allows the rescoring metric change to take effect.\n        if accuracy >= target_accuracy and bets_per_month >= 150:\n            # Maintain current thresholds; no adjustment this cycle\n            return\n\n        # If extremely few trades (or none), loosen to generate activity\n        if bets_per_month < 30.0:\n            self.min_confidence = max(0.5, self.min_confidence - 0.05)\n            self.min_models_agree = max(1, self.min_models_agree - 1)\n            # After loosening for low activity, skip further adjustments this cycle\n            self.min_models_agree = max(1, min(5, self.min_models_agree))\n            self.min_confidence = max(0.5, min(0.95, self.min_confidence))\n            return\n\n        # Primary: Sharpe and profitability\n        if sharpe < target_sharpe or profit_factor < target_profit_factor:\n            # Poor risk-adjusted/absolute performance: tighten to filter trades\n            self.min_confidence = min(0.9, self.min_confidence + 0.05)\n            self.min_models_agree = min(5, self.min_models_agree + 1)\n        elif accuracy < target_accuracy:\n            # Directional accuracy insufficient: tighten to require stronger agreement\n            self.min_confidence = min(0.9, self.min_confidence + 0.03)\n        elif bets_per_month < target_bets and accuracy >= target_accuracy:\n            # Too few trades despite decent accuracy: loosen thresholds\n            self.min_confidence = max(0.5, self.min_confidence - 0.02)\n            self.min_models_agree = max(1, self.min_models_agree - 1)\n        # else: keep thresholds stable\n\n        # Clamp to reasonable ranges\n        self.min_models_agree = max(1, min(5, self.min_models_agree))\n        self.min_confidence = max(0.5, min(0.95, self.min_confidence))\n\n    def get_params(self) -> dict:\n        return {\n            \"min_models_agree\": self.min_models_agree,\n            \"min_confidence\": self.min_confidence\n        }\n","numLines":149,"startLine":1,"totalLines":149}}}
